<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=basketball&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/basketball" class="extiw" title="w:basketball">basketball</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/basketball" class="extiw" title="w:basketball">Wikipedia </a></span></div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=basketball&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/basket#English" title="basket">basket</a></i> +‎ <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ball#English" title="ball">ball</a></i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=basketball&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈbɑːs.kɪt.bɔːl/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈbæs.kɪt.bɔl/</span>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cot%E2%80%93caught_merger" class="extiw" title="w:Cot–caught merger"><i>cot</i>–<i>caught</i> merger</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈbæs.kɪt.bɑl/</span></li></ul></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=basketball&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">basketball</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/basketballs#English" title="basketballs">basketballs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/sports" title="sports">sports</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/sport" title="sport">sport</a> in which two opposing teams of five players strive to put a <a href="/wiki/ball" title="ball">ball</a> through a <a href="/wiki/hoop" title="hoop">hoop</a>.
<span class="nyms-toggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonyms&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hoops#English" title="hoops">hoops</a></span>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/b-ball#English" title="b-ball">b-ball</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">play <b>basketball</b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The particular kind of <a href="/wiki/ball" title="ball">ball</a> used in the sport of basketball.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=basketball&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">basketball</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/basketballs#English" title="basketballs">basketballs</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/basketballing#English" title="basketballing">basketballing</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/w/index.php?title=basketballed&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="basketballed (page does not exist)">basketballed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To play basketball
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1968</b>,  Tom Tiede,  <cite>Coward</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">by high school he was <b>basketballing</b> with the best of an all-Negro league</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To <a href="/wiki/throw" title="throw">throw</a> in a similar way to when shooting a basketball
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1994</b>,  Jeff Probst,  <cite>Bachelor Butterflies</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He took a sip from a paper coffee-cup , crumpled it up and <b>basketballed</b> it into a small rubbish bin about five feet from him.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=basketball&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="da">basketball</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>singular definite</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-da def|s-form-of" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/basketballen#Danish" title="basketballen">basketballen</a></b>, <i>not used in plural form</i>)
